b'<?php\n// WordPress saves post meta values as \'longtext\' type \n// and hence, it makes it impossible to fetch the highest value based on a number.\n// So I came up with the following solution to get the highest value from the post meta\n\n// CHANGE [YOUR_META_KEY] with yours post meta key\nglobal $wpdb;\n$highest_val = $wpdb->get_var( "SELECT\n                                    meta_value\n                                FROM\n                                    wp_postmeta\n                                WHERE\n                                  meta_key = \'[YOUR_META_KEY]\'\n                                ORDER BY\n                                    CAST(meta_value AS UNSIGNED) DESC"\n                            );\n?>'

b'(function($){\r\n    $.fn.extend({\r\n        MyPagination: function(options) {\r\n            var defaults = {\r\n                height: 400,\r\n                fadeSpeed: 400\r\n            };\r\n            var options = $.extend(defaults, options);\r\n            //Creating a reference to the object\r\n            var objContent = $(this);\r\n            // other inner variables\r\n            var fullPages = new Array();\r\n            var subPages = new Array();\r\n            var height = 0;\r\n            var lastPage = 1;\r\n            var paginatePages;\r\n            // initialization function\r\n            init = function() {\r\n                objContent.children().each(function(i){\r\n                    if (height + this.clientHeight > options.height) {\r\n                        fullPages.push(subPages);\r\n                        subPages = new Array();\r\n                        height = 0;\r\n                    }\r\n                    height += this.clientHeight;\r\n                    subPages.push(this);\r\n                });\r\n                if (height > 0) {\r\n                    fullPages.push(subPages);\r\n                }\r\n                // wrapping each full page\r\n                $(fullPages).wrap("<div class=\'page\'></div>");\r\n                // hiding all wrapped pages\r\n                objContent.children().hide();\r\n                // making collection of pages for pagination\r\n                paginatePages = objContent.children();\r\n                // show first page\r\n                showPage(lastPage);\r\n                // draw controls\r\n                showPagination($(paginatePages).length);\r\n            };\r\n            // update counter function\r\n            updateCounter = function(i) {\r\n                $(\'#page_number\').html(i);\r\n            };\r\n            // show page function\r\n            showPage = function(page) {\r\n                i = page - 1;\r\n                if (paginatePages[i]) {\r\n                    // hiding old page, display new one\r\n                    $(paginatePages[lastPage]).fadeOut(options.fadeSpeed);\r\n                    lastPage = i;\r\n                    $(paginatePages[lastPage]).fadeIn(options.fadeSpeed);\r\n                    // and updating counter\r\n                    updateCounter(page);\r\n                }\r\n            };\r\n            // show pagination function (draw switching numbers)\r\n            showPagination = function(numPages) {\r\n                var pagins = \'\';\r\n                for (var i = 1; i <= numPages; i++) {\r\n                    pagins += \'<li><a href="#" onclick="showPage(\' + i + \'); return false;">\' + i + \'</a></li>\';\r\n                }\r\n                $(\'.pagination li:first-child\').after(pagins);\r\n            };\r\n            // perform initialization\r\n            init();\r\n            // and binding 2 events - on clicking to Prev\r\n            $(\'.pagination #prev\').click(function() {\r\n                showPage(lastPage);\r\n            });\r\n            // and Next\r\n            $(\'.pagination #next\').click(function() {\r\n                showPage(lastPage+2);\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n    });\r\n})(jQuery);\r\n// custom initialization\r\njQuery(window).load(function() {\r\n    $(\'#content\').MyPagination({height: 400, fadeSpeed: 400});\r\n});'

b'package main\n\nimport (\n    "fmt"\n    "flag"\n)\n\nvar (\n    // Set the following to anything higher than 0 and it will deadlock\n    maxdepth = flag.Int("depth", 0, "Reentrance depth")\n)\n\ntype Command struct {\n    depth int\n    result chan bool\n}\n\nfunc ree() chan Command {\n    reentrant_command := make(chan Command)\n\n    // This closure will handle the commands\n    go func() {\n        for cmd := range reentrant_command {\n            // This closure handles the individual command\n            go func() {\n                fmt.Printf("DEBUG - %#v - process\\n", cmd)\n                depth := cmd.depth\n                if depth < *maxdepth {\n                    result := make(chan bool)\n                    next := Command{depth + 1, result}\n                    reentrant_command <- next\n                    <-result\n                }\n                cmd.result <- true\n                fmt.Printf("DEBUG - %#v - complete\\n", cmd)\n            }()\n        }\n    }()\n\n    // Return the commanding channel\n    return reentrant_command\n}\n\nfunc main() { \n    flag.Parse()\n\n    send_cmd := ree()\n    cmd := Command{0, make(chan bool)}\n\n    fmt.Printf("DEBUG - %#v - send\\n", cmd)\n    send_cmd <- cmd\n    <-cmd.result\n    fmt.Printf("DEBUG - %#v - recv\\n", cmd)\n}'
